len(chocolate_tables),\n    \'research_themes\': dict(theme_counts),\n    \'detailed_table_data\': table_data,\n    \'analysis_timestamp\': pd.Timestamp.now().isoformat()\n}\n\nwith     "code": 'import requests\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\nimport os\nimport json\nfrom datetime import datetime\nimport re\nimport time\n\nprint("=== SEARCHING FOR TRANS FATTY ACID CHOCOLATE RESEARCH PAPER ===\\n")\nprint("Target: \'Trans fatty acid contents in chocolates and chocolate wafers in Turkey\'")\nprint("Objective: Retrieve full text and extract complete bibliography/reference list\\n")\n\n# Ensure workspace directory exists\nworkspace_dir = \'workspace\'\nos.makedirs(workspace_dir, exist_ok=True)\n\n# Define search strategies for finding the paper\nsearch_strategies = [\n    {\n        \'name\': \'Google Scholar Direct Search\',\n        \'query\': \'"Trans fatty acid contents in chocolates and chocolate wafers in Turkey"\',\n        \'search_engine\': \'scholar.google.com\'\n    },\n    {\n        \'name\': \'PubMed Search\',\n        \'query\': \'trans fatty acid chocolate wafer Turkey\',\n        \'search_engine\': \'pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov\'\n    },\n    {\n        \'name\': \'General Academic Search\',\n        \'query\': \'trans fatty acid chocolate Turkey research paper\',\n        \'search_engine\': \'google.com\'\n    },\n    {\n        \'name\': \'ResearchGate Search\',\n        \'query\': \'"trans fatty acid" chocolate wafer Turkey\',\n        \'search_engine\': \'researchgate.net\'\n    }\n]\n\nprint("=== STEP 1: SYSTEMATIC PAPER SEARCH ===\\n")\n\n# Start with Google Scholar as it\'s most likely to have academic papers\nprint("Starting with Google Scholar search...")\n\n# Use DuckDuckGo as a proxy to search Google Scholar\nsearch_results = []\n\nfor strategy in search_strategies:\n    print(f"\\n--- {strategy[\'name\']} ---")\n    print(f"Query: {strategy[\'query\']}")\n    \n    try:\n        # Use DuckDuckGo to search for the paper\n        search_url = "https://duckduckgo.com/html/"\n        \n        # Construct search query targeting specific search engine\n        if \'scholar.google.com\' in strategy[\'search_engine\']:\n            full_query = f"site:scholar.google.com {strategy[\'query\']}"\n        elif \'pubmed\' in strategy[\'search_engine\']:\n            full_query = f"site:pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov {strategy[\'query\']}"\n        elif \'researchgate\' in strategy[\'search_engine\']:\n            full_query = f"site:researchgate.net {strategy[\'query\']}"\n        else:\n            full_query = strategy[\'query\']\n        \n        params = {\n            \'q\': full_query,\n            \'kl\': \'us-en\'\n        }\n        \n        headers = {\n            \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36\'\n        }\n        \n        print(f"Searching: {full_query}")\n        response = requests.get(search_url, params=params, headers=headers, timeout=15)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        \n        print(f"Search response received (Status: {response.status_code})")\n        \n        # Parse search results\n        soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, \'html.parser\')\n        \n        # Find search result links\n        result_links = soup.find_all(\'a\', {\'class\': \'result__a\'})\n        \n        strategy_results = []\n        \n        for i, link in enumerate(result_links[:10], 1):  # Top 10 results\n            title = link.get_text().strip()\n            url = link.get(\'href\', \'\')\n            \n            print(f"  {i}. {title[:80]}{\'...\' if len(title) > 80 else \'\'}")\n            print(f"     URL: {url}")\n            \n            # Score relevance based on title content\n            title_lower = title.lower()\n            relevance_score = 0\n            \n            if \'trans fatty acid\' in title_lower:\n                relevance_score += 10\n            if \'chocolate\' in title_lower:\n                relevance_score += 8\n            if \'wafer\' in title_lower:\n                relevance_score += 6\n            if \'turkey\' in title_lower:\n                relevance_score += 5\n            if \'content\' in title_lower:\n                relevance_score += 3\n            \n            print(f"     Relevance Score: {relevance_score}")\n            \n            strategy_results.append({\n                \'title\': title,\n                \'url\': url,\n                \'relevance_score\': relevance_score,\n                \'search_strategy\': strategy[\'name\']\n            })\n        \n        search_results.extend(strategy_results)\n        print(f"Found {len(strategy_results)} results for this strategy")\n        \n        # Add delay between searches to be respectful\n        time.sleep(2)\n        \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f"Error with {strategy[\'name\']}: {e}")\n        continue\n\nprint(f"\\n=== STEP 2: ANALYZING SEARCH RESULTS ===\\n")\nprint(f"Total search results collected: {len(search_results)}")\n\n# Sort by relevance score\nsearch_results.sort(key=lambda x: x[\'relevance_score\'], reverse=True)\n\nprint("\\nTop 10 most relevant results:")\nfor i, result in enumerate(search_results[:10], 1):\n    print(f"\\n{i}. SCORE: {result[\'relevance_score\']}")\n    print(f"   Title: {result[\'title\']}")\n    print(f"   URL: {result[\'url\']}")\n    print(f"   Strategy: {result[\'search_strategy\']}")\n\n# Save search results\nsearch_data = {\n    \'search_timestamp\': datetime.now().isoformat(),\n    \'target_paper\': \'Trans fatty acid contents in chocolates and chocolate wafers in Turkey\',\n    \'search_strategies\': search_strategies,\n    \'total_results\': len(search_results),\n    \'results\': search_results\n}\n\nsearch_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'paper_search_results.json\')\nwith open(search_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    json.dump(search_data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)\n\nprint(f"\\nSearch results saved to: {search_file}")\n\n# Try to access the most promising results\nprint(f"\\n=== STEP 3: ATTEMPTING TO ACCESS TOP RESULTS ===\\n")\n\nhigh_relevance_results = [r for r in search_results if r[\'relevance_score\'] >= 15]\n\nif high_relevance_results:\n    print(f"Found {len(high_relevance_results)} high-relevance results (score >= 15)")\n    \n    for i, result in enumerate(high_relevance_results[:3], 1):  # Try top 3\n        print(f"\\n--- Attempting to access result {i} ---")\n        print(f"Title: {result[\'title\']}")\n        print(f"URL: {result[\'url\']}")\n        \n        try:\n            headers = {\n                \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36\'\n            }\n            \n            response = requests.get(result[\'url\'], headers=headers, timeout=20)\n            response.raise_for_status()\n            \n            print(f"Successfully accessed (Status: {response.status_code})")\n            print(f"Content length: {len(response.content):,} bytes")\n            \n            # Parse the page content\n            soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, \'html.parser\')\n            \n            # Look for paper content indicators\n            page_text = soup.get_text().lower()\n            \n            # Check if this looks like the target paper\n            paper_indicators = [\n                \'trans fatty acid\' in page_text,\n                \'chocolate\' in page_text,\n                \'wafer\' in page_text,\n                \'turkey\' in page_text,\n                \'bibliography\' in page_text or \'references\' in page_text,\n                \'abstract\' in page_text\n            ]\n            \n            indicator_count = sum(paper_indicators)\n            print(f"Paper indicators found: {indicator_count}/6")\n            \n            if indicator_count >= 4:  # Strong match\n                print("*** STRONG MATCH - This appears to be the target paper! ***")\n                \n                # Save the full page content\n                paper_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, f\'potential_target_paper_{i}.html\')\n                with open(paper_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                    f.write(response.text)\n                \n                print(f"Full page content saved to: {paper_file}")\n                \n                # Try to extract bibliography/references section\n                print("\\nSearching for bibliography/references section...")\n                \n                # Look for reference sections\n                ref_patterns = [\n                    r\'references?\\s*(?:\\n|<br>|</h\\d>)\',\n                    r\'bibliography\\s*(?:\\n|<br>|</h\\d>)\',\n                    r\'cited\\s+literature\\s*(?:\\n|<br>|</h\\d>)\',\n                    r\'works\\s+cited\\s*(?:\\n|<br>|</h\\d>)\'\n                ]\n                \n                references_found = False\n                for pattern in ref_patterns:\n                    matches = re.finditer(pattern, response.text, re.IGNORECASE)\n                    for match in matches:\n                        print(f"Found potential references section at position {match.start()}")\n                        references_found = True\n                        break\n                    if references_found:\n                        break\n                \n                if references_found:\n                    print("References section detected in the paper!")\n                else:\n                    print("No clear references section found in initial scan")\n                \n                # This looks promising, continue with this result\n                break\n            \n            else:\n                print(f"Weak match ({indicator_count}/6 indicators) - continuing search")\n        \n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f"Error accessing result {i}: {e}")\n            continue\n        \n        # Use a different search approach - try Bing search\n        search_url = "https://www.bing.com/search"\n        \n        params = {\n            \'q\': query,\n            \'count\': 20,  # Get more results\n            \'first\': 1\n        }\n        \n        headers = {\n            \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/120.0.0.0 Safari/537.36\',\n            \'Accept\': \'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8\',\n            \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.5\',\n            \'Accept-Encoding\': \'gzip, deflate\',\n            \'Connection\': \'keep-alive\'\n        }\n        \n        print(f"Searching Bing for: {query}")\n        response = requests.get(search_url, params=params, headers=headers, timeout=20)\n        print(f"Response status: {response.status_code}")\n        \n        if response.status_code == 200:\n            soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, \'html.parser\')\n            \n            # Find Bing search results\n            result_items = soup.find_all(\'li\', class_=\'b_algo\')\n            \n            print(f"Found {len(result_items)} search results")\n            \n            query_results = []\n            \n            for i, item in enumerate(result_items, 1):\n                # Extract title\n                title_elem = item.find(\'h2\')\n                if title_elem:\n                    title_link = title_elem.find(\'a\')\n                    if title_link:\n                        title = title_link.get_text().strip()\n                        url = title_link.get(\'href\', \'\')\n                    else:\n                        title = title_elem.get_text().strip()\n                        url = \'\'\n                else:\n                    title = \'No title\'\n                    url = \'\'\n                \n                # Extract snippet\n                snippet_elem = item.find(\'p\') or item.find(\'div\', class_=\'b_caption\')\n                snippet = snippet_elem.get_text().strip() if snippet_elem else \'No snippet\'\n                \n                print(f"\\n  {i}. {title[:80]}{\'...\' if len(title) > 80 else \'\'}")\n                print(f"     URL: {url}")\n                print(f"     Snippet: {snippet[:150]}{\'...\' if len(snippet) > 150 else \'\'}")\n                \n                # Score relevance\n                combined_text = f"{title} {snippet} {url}".lower()\n                relevance_score = 0\n                matching_terms = []\n                \n                if \'trans fatty acid\' in combined_text:\n                    relevance_score += 15\n                    matching_terms.append(\'trans fatty acid\')\n                elif \'trans fat\' in combined_text:\n                    relevance_score += 10\n                    matching_terms.append(\'trans fat\')\n                \n                if \'chocolate\' in combined_text:\n                    relevance_score += 12\n                    matching_terms.append(\'chocolate\')\n                \n                if \'wafer\' in combined_text:\n                    relevance_score += 8\n                    matching_terms.append(\'wafer\')\n                \n                if \'turkey\' in combined_text or \'turkish\' in combined_text:\n                    relevance_score += 10\n                    matching_terms.append(\'Turkey/Turkish\')\n                \n                if \'content\' in combined_text or \'composition\' in combined_text:\n                    relevance_score += 5\n                    matching_terms.append(\'content/composition\')\n                \n                # Boost for academic sources\n                if any(domain in url.lower() for domain in [\'researchgate.net\', \'pubmed\', \'scholar.google\', \'academia.edu\', \'sciencedirect\', \'springer\', \'wiley\']):\n                    relevance_score += 8\n                    matching_terms.append(\'academic source\')\n                \n                # Boost for PDF files\n                if \'.pdf\' in url.lower() or \'filetype:pdf\' in query.lower():\n                    relevance_score += 6\n                    matching_terms.append(\'PDF document\')\n                \n                print(f"     Relevance Score: {relevance_score}")\n                if matching_terms:\n                    print(f"     Matching Terms: {\', \'.join(matching_terms)}")\n                \n                query_results.append({\n                    \'title\': title,\n                    \'url\': url,\n                    \'snippet\': snippet,\n                    \'relevance_score\': relevance_score,\n                    \'matching_terms\': matching_terms,\n                    \'query\': query,\n                    \'search_engine\': \'Bing\'\n                })\n            \n            search_results.extend(query_results)\n            print(f"\\nAdded {len(query_results)} results from this query")\n        \n        else:\n            print(f"Search failed with status code: {response.status_code}")\n    \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f"Error with query \'{query}\': {e}")\n        continue\n    \n    # Add delay between searches\n    time.sleep(3)\n\nprint(f"\\n=== STEP 2: ANALYZING ALL SEARCH RESULTS ===")\nprint(f"Total results collected: {len(search_results)}")\n\n# Sort by relevance score\nsearch_results.sort(key=lambda x: x[\'relevance_score\'], reverse=True)\n\nprint(f"\\nTop 15 most relevant results:")\nfor i, result in enumerate(search_results[:15], 1):\n    print(f"\\n{i}. SCORE: {result[\'relevance_score\']}")\n    print(f"   Title: {result[\'title\']}")\n    print(f"   URL: {result[\'url\']}")\n    print(f"   Terms: {\', \'.join(result[\'matching_terms\']) if result[\'matching_terms\'] else \'None\'}")\n    print(f"   Query: {result[\'query\']}")\n\n# Save comprehensive search results\nsearch_data = {\n    \'search_timestamp\': datetime.now().isoformat(),\n    \'target_paper\': \'Trans fatty acid contents in chocolates and chocolate wafers in Turkey\',\n    \'search_method\': \'Bing search with multiple query variations\',\n    \'total_results\': len(search_results),\n    \'queries_used\': search_queries,\n    \'results\': search_results\n}\n\nsearch_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'comprehensive_paper_search_results.json\')\nwith open(search_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    json.dump(search_data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)\n\nprint(f"\\nComprehensive search results saved to: {search_file}")\n\n# Identify high-potential results\nhigh_potential = [r for r in search_results if r[\'relevance_score\'] >= 20]\nprint(f"\\n=== HIGH-POTENTIAL RESULTS (Score >= 20): {len(high_potential)} ===")\n\nfor i, result in enumerate(high_potential, 1):\n    print(f"\\n{i}. SCORE: {result[\'relevance_score\']} - {result[\'title\']}")\n    print(f"   URL: {result[\'url\']}")\n    print(f"   Matching terms: {\', \'.join(result[\'matching_terms\'])}")\n\n# Try to access the most promising results\nprint(f"\\n=== STEP 3: ACCESSING TOP CANDIDATES ===")\n\nif high_potential:\n    for i, result in enumerate(high_potential[:3], 1):  # Try top 3 high-potential results\n        print(f"\\n--- Accessing Candidate {i} ---")\n        print(f"Title: {result[\'title\']}")\n        print(f"URL: {result[\'url\']}")\n        print(f"Score: {result[\'relevance_score\']}")\n        \n        if not result[\'url\'] or result[\'url\'].startswith(\'#\'):\n            print("Invalid URL - skipping")\n            continue\n        \n        try:\n            headers = {\n                \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/120.0.0.0 Safari/537.36\',\n                \'Accept\': \'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,*/*;q=0.8\',\n                \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.9\'\n            }\n            \n            print("Attempting to access...")\n            response = requests.get(result[\'url\'], headers=headers, timeout=25, allow_redirects=True)\n            print(f"Response: {response.status_code} - not the target paper")\n            \n            else:\n                print(f"Failed to access: HTTP {response.status_code}")\n        \n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f"Error accessing candidate {i}: {e}")\n            continue\n        \n        # Delay between requests\n        time.sleep(4)\n\nelse:\n    print("No high-potential results found.     "code": 'import os\nimport json\nimport requests\nfrom datetime import datetime\nimport urllib.parse\nimport base64\n\nprint("=== FIXED PDF ACCESS FOR TRANS FATTY ACID CHOCOLATE RESEARCH PAPER ===")\nprint("Strategy: Properly decode Bing redirect URLs to access actual PDF files")\nprint("Objective: Retrieve full text and extract bibliography/references\\n")\n\n# Ensure workspace directory exists\nworkspace_dir = \'workspace\'\nos.makedirs(workspace_dir, exist_ok=True)\n\n# Load the search results file\nsearch_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'comprehensive_paper_search_results.json\')\n\nif os.path.exists(search_file):\n    print(f"Loading search results from: {search_file}")\n    \n    with open(search_file, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n        search_data = json.load(f)\n    \n    results = search_data.get(\'results\', [])\n    print(f"Found {len(results)} search results to process")\n    \n    print("\\n=== IMPROVED PDF URL EXTRACTION ===")\n    \n    pdf_candidates = []\n    \n    for idx, result in enumerate(results, 1):\n        url = result.get(\'url\', \'\')\n        title = result.get(\'title\', \'\')\n        score = result.get(\'relevance_score\', 0)\n        terms = result.get(\'matching_terms\', [])\n        snippet = result.get(\'snippet\', \'\')\n        \n        # Look for PDF indicators in URL, title, or snippet\n        has_pdf_indicator = (\n            \'.pdf\' in url.lower() or \n            \'.pdf\' in title.lower() or \n            \'.pdf\' in snippet.lower() or\n            \'pdf\' in terms or\n            \'PDF document\' in terms\n        )\n        \n        if has_pdf_indicator and \'bing.com/ck/a\' in url:\n            print(f"\\n{idx}. Processing Bing redirect URL...")\n            print(f"   Title: {title[:80]}...")\n            print(f"   Score: {score}")\n            print(f"   Original URL: {url[:100]}...")\n            \n            try:\n                # Extract the \'u=\' parameter from Bing redirect URL\n                if \'&u=\' in url:\n                    # Get the encoded URL part\n                    url_parts = url.split(\'&u=\')\n                    if len(url_parts) > 1:\n                        encoded_part = url_parts[1].split(\'&\')[0]  # Get just the encoded URL\n                        \n                        print(f"   Encoded part: {encoded_part[:50]}...")\n                        \n                        # URL decode first\n                        try:\n                            decoded_url = urllib.parse.unquote(encoded_part)\n                            print(f"   After URL decode: {decoded_url[:80]}...")\n                            \n                            # Check if it starts with \'a1\' (base64-like encoding)\n                            if decoded_url.startswith(\'a1\'):\n                                print("   Detected base64-like encoding, attempting to decode...")\n                                try:\n                                    # Remove \'a1\' prefix and try base64 decode\n                                    b64_part = decoded_url[2:]  # Remove \'a1\' prefix\n                                    \n                                    # Add padding if needed\n                                    missing_padding = len(b64_part) % 4\n                                    if missing_padding:\n                                        b64_part += \'=\' * (4 - missing_padding)\n                                    \n                                    decoded_bytes = base64.b64decode(b64_part)\n                                    final_url = decoded_bytes.decode(\'utf-8\')\n                                    \n                                    print(f"   *** DECODED URL: {final_url}")\n                                    \n                                    # Verify it\'s a valid URL\n                                    if final_url.startswith(\'http\') and \'.pdf\' in final_url.lower():\n                                        pdf_candidates.append({\n                                            \'title\': title,\n                                            \'original_url\': url,\n                                            \'pdf_url\': final_url,\n                                            \'score\': score,\n                                            \'terms\': terms,\n                                            \'snippet\': snippet\n                                        })\n                                        print(f"    VALID PDF URL EXTRACTED!")\n                                    else:\n                                        print(f"    Decoded URL not valid or not PDF")\n                                        \n                                except Exception as b64_error:\n                                    print(f"   Base64 decode failed: {b64_error}")\n                                    # Try using the URL-decoded version as-is\n                                    if decoded_url.startswith(\'http\') and \'.pdf\' in decoded_url.lower():\n                                        pdf_candidates.append({\n                                            \'title\': title,\n                                            \'original_url\': url,\n                                            \'pdf_url\': decoded_url,\n                                            \'score\': score,\n                                            \'terms\': terms,\n                                            \'snippet\': snippet\n                                        })\n                                        print(f"    Using URL-decoded version as PDF URL")\n                            \n                            else:\n                                # Direct URL after decoding\n                                if decoded_url.startswith(\'http\') and \'.pdf\' in decoded_url.lower():\n                                    pdf_candidates.append({\n                                        \'title\': title,\n                                        \'original_url\': url,\n                                        \'pdf_url\': decoded_url,\n                                        \'score\': score,\n                                        \'terms\': terms,\n                                        \'snippet\': snippet\n                                    })\n                                    print(f"    Direct PDF URL after decoding!")\n                                else:\n                                    print(f"    Decoded URL not a PDF")\n                        \n                        except Exception as decode_error:\n                            print(f"   URL decode failed: {decode_error}")\n                \n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f"   Error processing URL: {e}")\n        \n        elif \'.pdf\' in url.lower() and not \'bing.com\' in url:\n            # Direct PDF URL (not through Bing redirect)\n            print(f"\\n{idx}. Direct PDF URL found:")\n            print(f"   Title: {title[:80]}...")\n            print(f"   Score: {score}")\n            print(f"   Direct PDF URL: {url}")\n            \n            pdf_candidates.append({\n                \'title\': title,\n                \'original_url\': url,\n                \'pdf_url\': url,\n                \'score\': score,\n                \'terms\': terms,\n                \'snippet\': snippet\n            })\n    \n    print(f"\\n=== TOTAL PDF CANDIDATES EXTRACTED: {len(pdf_candidates)} ===")\n    \n    if len(pdf_candidates) == 0:\n        print("\\n No PDF URLs could be extracted from search results.")\n        print("This might be due to:")\n        print("1. Complex Bing URL encoding that our decoder can\'t handle")\n        print("2. PDFs behind authentication/paywalls")\n        print("3. Search results pointing to abstract pages rather than direct PDFs")\n        \n        # Let\'s try a different approach - look for any high-scoring results\n        print("\\n=== ALTERNATIVE APPROACH: ANALYZING HIGH-SCORING RESULTS ===")\n        \n        high_score_results = [r for r in results if r.get(\'relevance_score\', 0) >= 50]\n        print(f"Found {len(high_score_results)} results with score >= 50")\n        \n        for i, result in enumerate(high_score_results[:5], 1):\n            print(f"\\n{i}. Score: {result.get(\'relevance_score\', 0)}")\n            print(f"   Title: {result.get(\'title\', \'\')[:80]}...")\n            print(f"   Snippet: {result.get(\'snippet\', \'\')[:100]}...")\n            print(f"   URL: {result.get(\'url\', \'\')[:100]}...")\n            \n            # Try to access these URLs directly to see what we get\n            try:\n                headers = {\n                    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/120.0.0.0 Safari/537.36\'\n                }\n                \n                print(f"   Attempting to access URL...")\n                response = requests.get(result.get(\'url\', \'\'), headers=headers, timeout=15, allow_redirects=True)\n                print(f"   Response: {response.status_code}, Content-Type: {response.headers.get(\'content-type\', \'Unknown\')}")\n                print(f"   Final URL: {response.url[:100]}...")\n                \n                # Check if we got redirected to a PDF\n                if \'.pdf\' in response.url.lower() or \'application/pdf\' in response.headers.get(\'content-type\', \'\').lower():\n                    print(f"   *** FOUND PDF VIA REDIRECT! ***")\n                    \n                    pdf_candidates.append({\n                        \'title\': result.get(\'title\', \'\'),\n                        \'original_url\': result.get(\'url\', \'\'),\n                        \'pdf_url\': response.url,\n                        \'score\': result.get(\'relevance_score\', 0),\n                        \'terms\': result.get(\'matching_terms\', []),\n                        \'snippet\': result.get(\'snippet\', \'\'),\n                        \'method\': \'redirect_discovery\'\n                    })\n                \n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f"   Error accessing URL: {e}")\n    \n    # Sort PDF candidates by score\n    pdf_candidates.sort(key=lambda x: x[\'score\'], reverse=True)\n    \n    print(f"\\n=== FINAL PDF CANDIDATES: {len(pdf_candidates)} ===")\n    \n    for i, candidate in enumerate(pdf_candidates, 1):\n        print(f"\\n{i}. Score: {candidate[\'score\']}")\n        print(f"   Title: {candidate[\'title\'][:80]}...")\n        print(f"   PDF URL: {candidate[\'pdf_url\'][:100]}...")\n        print(f"   Method: {candidate.get(\'method\', \'url_decode\')}")\n    \n    # Try to download the top PDF candidates\n    if pdf_candidates:\n        print(f"\\n=== ATTEMPTING TO DOWNLOAD TOP PDF CANDIDATES ===")\n        \n        successful_downloads = []\n        \n        for i, candidate in enumerate(pdf_candidates[:3], 1):  # Try top 3\n            print(f"\\n--- Downloading PDF Candidate {i} ---")\n            print(f"Title: {candidate[\'title\']}")\n            print(f"Score: {candidate[\'score\']}")\n            print(f"PDF URL: {candidate[\'pdf_url\']}")\n            \n            try:\n                headers = {\n                    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/120.0.0.0 Safari/537.36\',\n                    \'Accept\': \'application/pdf,application/octet-stream,*/*\',\n                    \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.9\'\n                }\n                \n                print("Attempting to download PDF...")\n                response = requests.get(candidate[\'pdf_url\'], headers=headers, timeout=30, allow_redirects=True)\n                print(f"Response: {response.status_code} - Content length: {len(response.content):,} bytes")\n                print(f"Content type: {response.headers.get(\'content-type\', \'Unknown\')}")\n                \n                if response.status_code == 200:\n                    # Check if it\'s actually a PDF\n                    content_type = response.headers.get(\'content-type\', \'\').lower()\n                    is_pdf = \'pdf\' in content_type or response.content.startswith(b\'%PDF\')\n                    \n                    if is_pdf and len(response.content) > 1000:  # Reasonable PDF size\n                        print("*** SUCCESS: Downloaded PDF content! ***")\n                        \n                        # Save the PDF\n                        pdf_filename = f"target_paper_candidate_{i}.pdf"\n                        pdf_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, pdf_filename)\n                        \n                        with open(pdf_path, \'wb\') as f:\n                            f.write(response.content)\n                        \n                        print(f"PDF saved to: {pdf_path}")\n                        print(f"PDF size: {len(response.content):,} bytes")\n                        \n                        # Save basic info about this successful download\n                        successful_downloads.append({\n                            \'candidate_num\': i,\n                            \'title\': candidate[\'title\'],\n                            \'pdf_path\': pdf_path,\n                            \'pdf_url\': candidate[\'pdf_url\'],\n                            \'score\': candidate[\'score\'],\n                            \'file_size\': len(response.content)\n                        })\n                        \n                        print(f"\\n CANDIDATE {i} SUCCESSFULLY DOWNLOADED!")\n                        \n                        # For now, just save the PDF - text extraction can be done in next step\n                        # if PyPDF2 is available\n                        \n                    else:\n                        print(f"Not a valid PDF or too small ({len(response.content)} bytes)")\n                        print(f"Content starts with: {response.content[:50]}")\n                \n                else:\n                    print(f"Failed to download: HTTP {response.status_code}")\n                    if response.content:\n                        print(f"Response content preview: {response.content[:200]}")\n            \n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f"Error downloading PDF candidate {i}: {e}")\n                continue\n        \n        # Summary\n        print(f"\\n=== DOWNLOAD SUMMARY ===")\n        print(f"Total PDF candidates found: {len(pdf_candidates)}")\n        print(f"Successful downloads: {len(successful_downloads)}")\n        \n        if successful_downloads:\n            print("\\nSuccessfully downloaded PDFs:")\n            for download in successful_downloads:\n                print(f"\\n{download[\'candidate_num\']}. {download[\'title\'][:60]}...")\n                print(f"   File: {download[\'pdf_path\']}")\n                print(f"   Size: {download[\'file_size\']:,} bytes")\n                print(f"   Score: {download[\'score\']}")\n            \n            print(f"\\n SUCCESS: Downloaded {len(successful_downloads)} PDF(s)!")\n            print(f"Next step: Extract text and bibliography from downloaded PDF(s).")\n        else:\n            print(f"\\n No successful PDF downloads.")\n        \n        # Save results\n        download_results = {\n            \'download_timestamp\': datetime.now().isoformat(),\n            \'total_pdf_candidates\': len(pdf_candidates),\n            \'successful_downloads\': len(successful_downloads),\n            \'pdf_candidates\': pdf_candidates,\n            \'successful_downloads\': successful_downloads\n        }\n        \n        results_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'fixed_pdf_download_results.json\')\n        with open(results_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n            json.dump(download_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)\n        \n        print(f"\\nDownload results saved to: {results_file}")\n    \n    else:\n        print(f"\\n No PDF candidates could be extracted or accessed.")\n        print(f"The target paper may be:")\n        print(f"1. Behind a paywall or institutional access")\n        print(f"2. Not freely available online")\n        print(f"3. Indexed but not directly accessible")\n        print(f"4. Requiring special access permissions")\n\nelse:\n    print(f"Search results file not found: {search_file}")\n    print("Please run the search phase first.")\n\nprint(f"\\n=== FIXED PDF ACCESS PHASE COMPLETE ===")',

    "code": 'import os\nimport json\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\nprint("=== MANUAL BIBLIOGRAPHY SEARCH IN EXTRACTED TEXT ===")\nprint("Objective: Manually search for references in the extracted text using alternative patterns")\nprint("Strategy: Examine the extracted text file and look for bibliography using different approaches\\n")\n\n# Ensure workspace directory exists\nworkspace_dir = \'workspace\'\nos.makedirs(workspace_dir, exist_ok=True)\n\n# First, let\'s inspect the extracted text file to understand its structure\ntext_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'extracted_text_pdf_1.txt\')\n\nif os.path.exists(text_file):\n    print(f"Found extracted text file: {text_file}")\n    \n    # Read the extracted text\n    with open(text_file, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n        full_text = f.read()\n    \n    print(f"Text file size: {len(full_text):,} characters")\n    \n    # Let\'s examine the structure by looking at page breaks and content\n    print("\\n=== EXAMINING TEXT STRUCTURE ===")\n    \n    # Split by page markers to understand the document structure\n    pages = full_text.split(\'--- PAGE\')\n    print(f"Document appears to have {len(pages)} sections (including header)")\n    \n    # Look at the last few pages where references are typically located\n    print("\\n=== EXAMINING FINAL PAGES FOR REFERENCES ===")\n    \n    for i, page in enumerate(pages[-3:], len(pages)-2):  # Last 3 pages\n        if \'PAGE\' in page:\n            page_num = page.split(\'---\')[0].strip()\n            page_content = page.split(\'---\')[1] if \'---\' in page else page\n            \n            print(f"\\n--- PAGE {page_num} CONTENT PREVIEW ---")\n            print(f"Length: {len(page_content)} characters")\n            print(f"First 300 characters: {page_content[:300]}...")\n            print(f"Last 300 characters: ...{page_content[-300:]}")\n    \n    # Search for alternative reference patterns\n    print("\\n=== SEARCHING FOR ALTERNATIVE REFERENCE PATTERNS ===")\n    \n    text_lower = full_text.lower()\n    \n    # Look for various patterns that might indicate references\n    reference_patterns = [\n        \'literature cited\',\n        \'cited literature\', \n        \'reference list\',\n        \'works cited\',\n        \'bibliography\',\n        \'references\',\n        \'ref.\',\n        \'literature\',\n        # Look for author-year patterns that might indicate references\n        r\'\\b[A-Z][a-z]+,?\\s+[A-Z]\\.?.*?\\(\\d{4}\\)\',\n        # Look for numbered reference patterns\n        r\'\\n\\s*\\d+\\.\\s+[A-Z]\',\n        # Look for journal citation patterns\n        r\'\\b[A-Z][a-z]+.*?\\d{4}.*?\\d+:\\d+\',\n    ]\n    \n    found_patterns = []\n    \n    for pattern in reference_patterns[:7]:  # Text patterns first\n        if pattern in text_lower:\n            positions = []\n            start = 0\n            while True:\n                pos = text_lower.find(pattern, start)\n                if pos == -1:\n                    break\n                positions.append(pos)\n                start = pos + 1\n            \n            if positions:\n                found_patterns.append({\n                    \'pattern\': pattern,\n                    \'positions\': positions,\n                    \'count\': len(positions)\n                })\n                print(f"\\nFound \'{pattern}\' at {len(positions)} position(s): {positions}")\n                \n                # Show context around each occurrence\n                for pos in positions[:3]:  # Show first 3 occurrences\n                    context_start = max(0, pos - 100)\n                    context_end = min(len(full_text), pos + len(pattern) + 200)\n                    context = full_text[context_start:context_end]\n                    print(f"  Context at position {pos}: ...{context}...")\n    \n    # Now try regex patterns for citation formats\n    import re\n    \n    print("\\n=== SEARCHING FOR CITATION PATTERNS ===")\n    \n    regex_patterns = [\n        (r\'\\b[A-Z][a-z]+,?\\s+[A-Z]\\.?.*?\\(\\d{4}\\)\', \'Author (Year) format\'),\n        (r\'\\n\\s*\\d+\\.\\s+[A-Z][a-z]+\', \'Numbered references\'),\n        (r\'\\b[A-Z][a-z]+.*?\\d{4}.*?\\d+:\\d+\', \'Journal citations\'),\n        (r\'\\b[A-Z][a-z]+.*?\\d{4}.*?pp?\\.?\\s*\\d+\', \'Page number citations\'),\n        (r\'\\([A-Z][a-z]+.*?\\d{4}\\)\', \'In-text citations\')\n    ]\n    \n    citation_matches = []\n    \n    for pattern, description in regex_patterns:\n        matches = re.findall(pattern, full_text)\n        if matches:\n            print(f"\\nFound {len(matches)} matches for {description}:")\n            for i, match in enumerate(matches[:5], 1):  # Show first 5\n                clean_match = \' \'.join(match.split())  # Clean whitespace\n                print(f"  {i}. {clean_match}")\n                citation_matches.append(clean_match)\n            \n            if len(matches) > 5:\n                print(f"  ... and {len(matches) - 5} more matches")\n    \n    # Look for specific sections that might contain references\n    print("\\n=== SEARCHING FOR POTENTIAL REFERENCE SECTIONS ===")\n    \n    # Split text into paragraphs and look for sections with multiple citations\n    paragraphs = full_text.split(\'\\n\\n\')\n    \n    potential_ref_sections = []\n    \n    for i, paragraph in enumerate(paragraphs):\n        if len(paragraph) > 100:  # Only consider substantial paragraphs\n            # Count citation-like patterns in this paragraph\n            citation_count = 0\n            citation_count += len(re.findall(r\'\\(\\d{4}\\)\', paragraph))  # Year patterns\n            citation_count += len(re.findall(r\'\\b[A-Z][a-z]+,\\s*[A-Z]\', paragraph))  # Author patterns\n            citation_count += len(re.findall(r\'\\d+:\\d+\', paragraph))  # Page patterns\n            \n            if citation_count >= 3:  # Paragraph with multiple citation indicators\n                potential_ref_sections.append({\n                    \'paragraph_index\': i,\n                    \'citation_count\': citation_count,\n                    \'length\': len(paragraph),\n                    \'content\': paragraph\n                })\n    \n    if potential_ref_sections:\n        print(f"Found {len(potential_ref_sections)} paragraphs with multiple citation patterns:")\n        \n        # Sort by citation density\n        potential_ref_sections.sort(key=lambda x: x[\'citation_count\'], reverse=True)\n        \n        for i, section in enumerate(potential_ref_sections[:3], 1):  # Show top 3\n            print(f"\\n{i}. Paragraph {section[\'paragraph_index\']} - {section[\'citation_count\']} citations, {section[\'length\']} chars")\n            print(f"   Preview: {section[\'content\'][:200]}...")\n    \n    # Try to find the actual references by looking at the end of the document\n    print("\\n=== EXAMINING END OF DOCUMENT FOR REFERENCES ===")\n    \n    # Look at the last 3000 characters of the document\n    end_section = full_text[-3000:]\n    print(f"Last 3000 characters of document:")\n    print(f"Content: {end_section}")\n    \n    # Look for any structured list at the end\n    lines = end_section.split(\'\\n\')\n    structured_lines = []\n    \n    for line in lines:\n        line = line.strip()\n        if line and (line[0].isdigit() or re.match(r\'^[A-Z][a-z]+\', line)):\n            structured_lines.append(line)\n    \n    if structured_lines:\n        print(f"\\nFound {len(structured_lines)} potentially structured reference lines:")\n        for i, line in enumerate(structured_lines[:10], 1):\n            print(f"  {i}. {line}")\n        \n        # Save these as potential references\n        if len(structured_lines) >= 5:  # Only if we have a reasonable number\n            ref_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'manual_extracted_references.txt\')\n            with open(ref_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                f.write(f"MANUALLY EXTRACTED REFERENCES\\n")\n                f.write(f"Source: Trans fatty acid contents in chocolates and chocolate wafers in Turkey\\n")\n                f.write(f"Extraction Date: {datetime.now().isoformat()}\\n")\n                f.write(f"Method: Manual pattern search\\n")\n                f.write(f"Total References Found: {len(structured_lines)}\\n")\n                f.write("=" * 80 + "\\n\\n")\n                \n                for i, line in enumerate(structured_lines, 1):\n                    f.write(f"{i}. {line}\\n")\n            \n            print(f"\\n REFERENCES SAVED TO: {ref_file}")\n    \n    # Create a comprehensive search summary\n    search_summary = {\n        \'search_date\': datetime.now().isoformat(),\n        \'source_file\': text_file,\n        \'total_text_length\': len(full_text),\n        \'patterns_searched\': len(reference_patterns),\n        \'patterns_found\': len(found_patterns),\n        \'citation_matches\': len(citation_matches),\n        \'potential_ref_sections\': len(potential_ref_sections),\n        \'structured_lines_found\': len(structured_lines) if \'structured_lines\' in locals() else 0,\n        \'search_results\': {\n            \'found_patterns\': found_patterns,\n            \'citation_samples\': citation_matches[:20] if citation_matches else [],\n            \'potential_sections\': [s[\'content\'][:200] for s in potential_ref_sections[:3]] if potential_ref_sections else []\n        }\n    }\n    \n    summary_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'manual_bibliography_search_results.json\')\n    with open(summary_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n        json.dump(search_summary, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)\n    \n    print(f"\\n SEARCH SUMMARY SAVED TO: {summary_file}")\n    \n    # Final assessment\n    if \'structured_lines\' in locals() and len(structured_lines) >= 5:\n        print(f"\\n SUCCESS: Found {len(structured_lines)} potential references")\n        print(f"References have been extracted and saved for matching with Excel table titles")\n    else:\n        print(f"\\n LIMITED SUCCESS: Found some citation patterns but no clear reference list")\n        print(f"The paper may use a non-standard reference format or embed references differently")\n        print(f"Manual review of the extracted text may be needed")\n\nelse:\n    print(f"Extracted text file not found: {text_file}")\n    print("Please run the PDF text extraction phase first.")\n\nprint(f"\\n=== MANUAL BIBLIOGRAPHY SEARCH COMPLETE ===")',

Read the file to understand its structure\n    print("\\n=== INSPECTING MANUAL REFERENCES FILE STRUCTURE ===")\n    with open(manual_refs_file, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n        refs_content = f.read()\n    \n    print(f"Content length: {len(refs_content):,} characters")\n    print(f"\\nFirst 500 characters:")\n    print(refs_content[:500])\n    print(f"\\nLast 500 characters:")\n    print(refs_content[-500:])\n    \n    # Split into lines and examine the structure\n    lines = refs_content.split(\'\\n\')\n    print(f"\\nTotal lines in file: {len(lines)}")\n    \n    # Find where the actual references start (after the header)\n    ref_start_idx = 0\n    for i, line in enumerate(lines):\n        if line.strip().startswith(\'1.\') or (line.strip() and line.strip()[0].isdigit()):\n            ref_start_idx = i\n            break\n        elif \'=\' * 50 in line:  # Skip empty lines and separators\n            reference_lines.append(line)\n    \n    print(f"\\nExtracted {len(reference_lines)} reference lines")\n    print("\\nFirst 10 reference lines:")\n    for i, ref in enumerate(reference_lines[:10], 1):\n        print(f"  {i}. {ref}")\n    \n    # Look for the references section in the full text\n        # Based on the previous output, we know the references are at the end\n        text_lower = full_text.lower()\n        \n        # Find the start of references by looking for the first author citation\n        # From the output, we can see references start with author names\n        import re\n        \n        # Look for the pattern that indicates start of references\n        # Based on the output, references seem to start after the main text\n        \n        # Let\'s find where the references section actually begins\n        # Look for the transition from main text to references\n        ref_start_patterns = [\n            \'katan m.b\',  # First reference we saw in the output\n            \'ascherio a\',  # Another early reference\n            \'ayagari a\',   # Another reference pattern\n        ]\n        \n        ref_start_pos = -1\n        for pattern in ref_start_patterns:\n            pos = text_lower.find(pattern)\n            if pos != -1:\n                ref_start_pos = pos\n                break\n        \n        if ref_start_pos != -1:\n            print(f"Found references starting at position {ref_start_pos}")\n            \n            # (year):" or "Author A.B., Author C.D. (year):"\n            ref_pattern = r\'([A-Z][a-z]+\\s+[A-Z](?:\\.[A-Z])?(?:,\\s+[A-Z][a-z]+\\s+[A-Z](?:\\.[A-Z])?)*(?:,\\s+[A-Z][a-z]+\\s+[A-Z](?:\\.[A-Z])?)*\\.?\\s*\\(\\d{4}\\)[^\\n]*(?:\\n[^A-Z\\n][^\\n]*)*?)(?=\\n[A-Z][a-z]+\\s+[A-Z]|$)\'\n            \n            matches = re.findall(ref_pattern, refs_section, re.MULTILINE | re.DOTALL)\n            \n            if matches:\n                print(f"\\nFound {len(matches)} complete references using regex pattern:")\n                \n                for i, match in enumerate(matches[:10], 1):  # Show first 10\n                    clean_ref = \' \'.join(match.split())  # Clean whitespace\n                    individual_refs.append(clean_ref)\n                    print(f"  {i}. {clean_ref[:100]}...")\n                \n                if len(matches) > 10:\n                    print(f"  ... and {len(matches) - 10} more references")\n                    # Add the rest\n                    for match in matches[10:]:\n                        clean_ref = \' \'.join(match.split())\n                        individual_refs.append(clean_ref)\n            \n            else:\n                print("Regex pattern didn\'t work, trying line-by-line approach...")\n                \n                # Alternative approach: split by lines and group related lines\n                lines = refs_section.split(\'\\n\')\n                current_ref = ""\n                \n                for line in lines:\n                    line = line.strip()\n                    if not line:\n                        continue\n                    \n                    # Check if this line starts a new reference (author name pattern)\n                    if re.match(r\'^[A-Z][a-z]+\\s+[A-Z]\', line):\n                        # Save previous reference if it exists\n                        if current_ref:\n                            clean_ref = \' \'.join(current_ref.split())\n                            if len(clean_ref) > 20:  # Only substantial references\n                                individual_refs.append(clean_ref)\n                        current_ref = line\n                    else:\n                        # Continuation of current reference\n                        current_ref += " " + line\n                \n                # Don\'t forget the last reference\n                if current_ref:\n                    clean_ref = \' \'.join(current_ref.split())\n                    if len(clean_ref) > 20:\n                        individual_refs.append(clean_ref)\n                \n                print(f"\\nExtracted {len(individual_refs)} references using line-by-line approach")\n            \n            # Save the cleaned, complete bibliography\n            if individual_refs:\n                final_refs_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'complete_bibliography_trans_fatty_acid_paper.txt\')\n                with open(final_refs_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                    f.write("COMPLETE BIBLIOGRAPHY - TRANS FATTY ACID CONTENTS IN CHOCOLATES AND CHOCOLATE WAFERS IN TURKEY\\n")\n                    f.write("Source Paper: akmak, Y.S., Gler, G.., Aktmsek, A. Categorize files by type\n    excel_files = [f for f in workspace_files if f.endswith((\'.xlsx\', \'.xls\', \'.csv\'))]\n    json_files = [f for f in workspace_files if f.endswith(\'.json\')]\n    txt_files = [f for f in workspace_files if f.endswith(\'.txt\')]\n    pdf_files = [f for f in workspace_files if f.endswith(\'.pdf\')]\n    \n    print(f"\\nFile categories:")\n    print(f"  Excel/CSV files: {len(excel_files)} - {excel_files}")\n    print(f"  JSON files: {len(json_files)} - {json_files[:5]}{\'...\' if len(json_files) > 5 else \'\'}")\n    print(f"  Text files: {len(txt_files)} - {txt_files[:5]}{\'...\' if len(txt_files) > 5 else \'\'}")\n    print(f"  PDF files: {len(pdf_files)} - {pdf_files}")\n    \n    # in title_lower:\n        key_terms = [\'oil\', \'fat\', \'composition\', \'fatty acid\', \'vegetable\', \'animal\']\n    elif \'cholesterol\' in title_lower or \'hdl\' in title_lower or \'serum\' in for ref_idx, reference in enumerate(references, 1):\n        ref_lower = reference.lower()\n        match_score = 0\n        matching_terms = []\n        \n        # Count how many key terms appear in this reference\n        for term in key_terms:\n            if term in ref_lower:\n                match_score += 1\n                matching_terms.append(term)\n        \n        if match_score > 0:\n            potential_matches.append({\n                \'ref_number\': ref_idx,\n                \'reference\': reference,\n                \'match_score\': match_score,\n                \'matching_terms\': matching_terms\n            })\n    \n    # Sort by match score\n    potential_matches.sort(key=lambda x: x[\'match_score\'], reverse=True)\n    \n    print(f"Found {match[\'matching_terms\']}")\n        print(f"    {match[\'reference\'][:80]}...")\n    \n    # Store the best match (or indicate no match found)\n    best_match = potential_matches[0] if potential_matches else None\n    \n    matching_results.append({\n        \'table_number\': i,\n        \'table_title\': table_title,\n        \'best_match_ref_number\': best_match[\'ref_number\'] if \'all_potential_matches\': potential_matches\n    })\n    \n    if best_match:\n        print(f"   BEST MATCH: Reference #{best_match[\'ref_number\']} (Score: {best_match[\'match_score\']})")\n        print(f"    Reference #{ref_num}: {result[\'best_match_reference\'][:60]}...")\n        reference_numbers.append(str(ref_num))\n    else:\n        print(f"    No match found")\n
